+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Script to reproduce the dynamic filter pushdown issue."""
+
+import os
+import subprocess
+import tempfile
+import sys
+
+def run_sql_test():
+    """Run SQL test to reproduce the issue."""
+    
+    # Create temporary directory for test files
+    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
+        # Create test data
+        t1_path = os.path.join(tmpdir, "t1.parquet")
+        t2_path = os.path.join(tmpdir, "t2.parquet")
+        
+        # Create a simple test script using datafusion-cli
+        test_script = f"""
+        CREATE EXTERNAL TABLE t1 STORED AS PARQUET LOCATION '{t1_path}';
+        CREATE EXTERNAL TABLE t2 STORED AS PARQUET LOCATION '{t2_path}';
+        
+        -- Test 1: Normal case (t1 small, t2 large with filter)
+        EXPLAIN ANALYZE SELECT * FROM t1 JOIN t2 ON t1.k = t2.k WHERE t2.v = 1000000;
+        
+        -- Test 2: Swapped case (t2 side larger with more restrictive filter)
+        EXPLAIN ANALYZE SELECT * FROM t1 JOIN t2 ON t1.k = t2.k WHERE t2.v >= 1000000;
+        """
+        
+        script_path = os.path.join(tmpdir, "test.sql")
+        with open(script_path, "w") as f:
+            f.write(test_script)
+        
+        # Run the test using datafusion-cli
+        print("Running test to reproduce the issue...")
+        try:
+            # First build the datafusion-cli if needed
+            subprocess.run(["cargo", "build", "--bin", "datafusion"], 
+                         cwd="/testbed/repo", check=True)
+            
+            # Run the test
+            result = subprocess.run([
+                "/testbed/repo/target/debug/datafusion",
+                "--data-dir", tmpdir,
+                "-f", script_path
+            ], capture_output=True, text=True)
+            
+            print("STDOUT:")
+            print(result.stdout)
+            if result.stderr:
+                print("STDERR:")
+                print(result.stderr)
+            
+            return result.returncode == 0
+            
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Error running test: {e}")
+            return False
+
+def main():
+    # First, let's check if we need to generate test data
+    print("Starting issue reproduction...")
+    
+    # The issue is about the logic in filter pushdown, so let's create a simpler test
+    # that demonstrates the problem without needing actual data files
+    
+    # Let's examine the problematic code more closely
+    print("\n1. Analyzing the issue in HashJoinExec...")
+    
+    # Read the relevant part of the file
+    hash_join_file = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/physical-plan/src/joins/hash_join.rs"
+    with open(hash_join_file, "r") as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    # Find the problematic section
+    import re
+    
+    # Look for the filter pushdown implementation
+    problem_pattern = r"Add actual dynamic filter to right side.*?right_child = right_child\.with_self_filter\(dynamic_filter\)"
+    match = re.search(problem_pattern, content, re.DOTALL)
+    
+    if match:
+        print("\nFound the problematic code section:")
+        print("-" * 60)
+        print(match.group(0))
+        print("-" * 60)
+        
+        print("\nThe issue: Dynamic filter is always applied to the 'right' side (probe side)")
+        print("But when the join order is swapped, the dynamic filter should be applied to the build side")
+        print("Currently, it's applied to the probe side regardless of which table is actually larger.")
+    
+    # Let's also check how the dynamic filter is created
+    create_filter_pattern = r"fn create_dynamic_filter.*?Arc::new\(DynamicFilterPhysicalExpr::new\(right_keys, lit\(true\)\)\)"
+    match = re.search(create_filter_pattern, content, re.DOTALL)
+    
+    if match:
+        print("\nDynamic filter creation logic:")
+        print("-" * 60)
+        print(match.group(0))
+        print("-" * 60)
+        print("\nThe dynamic filter is created using right_keys from the join ON clause")
+        print("This means it's designed to filter the probe side, but the issue is about")
+        print("which table actually becomes the probe side after join order optimization.")
+    
+    print("\n2. Verifying the issue with a simpler approach...")
+    
+    # Let's look for test files that might help us understand the expected behavior
+    test_files = [
+        "/testbed/repo/datafusion/core/tests/physical_optimizer/filter_pushdown/mod.rs",
+        "/testbed/repo/datafusion/physical-optimizer/src/filter_pushdown.rs"
+    ]
+    
+    for test_file in test_files:
+        if os.path.exists(test_file):
+            print(f"\nFound test file: {test_file}")
+            with open(test_file, "r") as f:
+                test_content = f.read()
+                if "dynamic filter" in test_content.lower():
+                    print("  Contains dynamic filter tests")
+    
+    print("\n3. Conclusion:")
+    print("The issue is that when the join order is swapped (smaller table becomes build side),")
+    print("the dynamic filter pushdown logic still applies the filter to the right side (probe side)")
+    print("instead of correctly identifying which side should be filtered.")
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Analyze the actual solution for dynamic filter pushdown."""
+
+def analyze_solution():
+    print("=== REANALYSIS OF THE PROBLEM ===\n")
+    
+    print("After careful examination, the issue is NOT in swap_inputs().")
+    print("The dynamic filter creation is actually CORRECT.")
+    print("\nThe REAL ISSUE is in how filters are pushed down.\n")
+    
+    print("Current logic in gather_filters_for_pushdown():")
+    print("  'Add actual dynamic filter to right side (probe side)'")
+    print("  This assumes the RIGHT side is ALWAYS the probe side")
+    print("  But after swap, the RIGHT side becomes the original LEFT side\n")
+    
+    print("=== EXAMPLE ===")
+    print("Original query: SELECT * FROM t1 JOIN t2 ON t1.k = t2.k WHERE t2.v >= 1000000")
+    print("After optimization:")
+    print("- t2.v >= 1000000 reduces t2 from 10M to 9M rows")
+    print("- t1 has 1M rows")
+    print("- t2 (9M) > t1 (1M), so join gets SWAPPED")
+    print("- t2 becomes LEFT (build side)")
+    print("- t1 becomes RIGHT (probe side)")
+    print("\nDynamic filter created using RIGHT keys from swapped ON:")
+    print("- ON(t2.k, t1.k) -> right key = t1.k")
+    print("- Filter will be: t1.k >= min(t2.k) AND t1.k <= max(t2.k)")
+    print("- This should reduce t1 scan based on actual t2.k values")
+    
+    print("\n=== BUT THE ISSUE IS ELSEWHERE ===")
+    print("Looking at the PR description again:")
+    print("- 'DynamicFilterPhysicalExpr [ k@0 >= 3 AND k@0 <= 999998 ]'")
+    print("- Here k@0 refers to t2.k (not t1.k)")
+    print("- This suggests the filter is being applied to the WRONG table\n")
+    
+    print("=== ACTUAL FIX NEEDED ===")
+    print("The dynamic filter expressions reference COLUMN INDICES, not names.")
+    print("After swap, the column references need to be RE-MAPPED correctly.")
+    print("\nThe fix should be:")
+    print("1. In swap_inputs(), when we swap ON clauses, we also need to")
+    print("   ensure dynamic filter expressions reference the correct columns.")
+    print("2. The DynamicFilterPhysicalExpr needs to update its references")
+    print("   based on the new schema after swap.\n")
+    
+    print("=== SIMPLER FIX ===")
+    print("Actually, the issue might be more fundamental:")
+    print("The dynamic filter ALWAYS filters the column(s) referenced in its children.")
+    print("These children are defined when create_dynamic_filter() is called.")
+    print("After swap, the old dynamic filter still references the original columns.")
+    print("\nWe need to CREATE A NEW dynamic filter after swap with correct column references.")
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    analyze_solution()

+    println!("- After swap: t2 (left) JOIN t1 (right) ON t2.k = t1.k");

+

+    println!("4. This should be correct: new right = original left, so keys are correct");
